	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Google Books</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Service from Google</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">"Google Print" redirects here. It is not to be confused with <a href="/wiki/Google_Cloud_Print" title="Google Cloud Print">Google Cloud Print</a>.</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This article is about Google's book search engine. For Google's e-book service, see <a href="/wiki/Google_Play_Books" title="Google Play Books">Google Play Books</a>. For the children's book, see <a href="/wiki/The_Google_Book" title="The Google Book">The Google Book</a>.</div>
<table class="infobox vcard" style="width:22em"><caption class="fn org">Google Books</caption><tbody><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><a href="/wiki/File:Google_Books_logo_2015.svg" class="image"><img alt="Google Books logo 2015.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Google_Books_logo_2015.svg/250px-Google_Books_logo_2015.svg.png" decoding="async" width="250" height="86" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Google_Books_logo_2015.svg/375px-Google_Books_logo_2015.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Google_Books_logo_2015.svg/500px-Google_Books_logo_2015.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="506" data-file-height="174" /></a></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" style="box-sizing:border-box;width:100%;font-size:95%;padding:4px;border:none;"><div style="font-size:100%;line-height:1.6;font-weight:bold;background:transparent;text-align:left;;background:gainsboro;text-align:center">Screenshot</div><div class="mw-collapsible-content" style="background:transparent;text-align:left;;text-align:center">
<a href="/wiki/File:Google_books_screenshot.png" class="image"><img alt="Google books screenshot.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/aa/Google_books_screenshot.png/250px-Google_books_screenshot.png" decoding="async" width="250" height="123" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/aa/Google_books_screenshot.png/375px-Google_books_screenshot.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/a/aa/Google_books_screenshot.png 2x" data-file-width="450" data-file-height="221" /></a><div></div></div></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><div style="padding:0.1em 0;line-height:1.2em;">Type of site</div></th><td><a href="/wiki/Digital_library" title="Digital library">Digital library</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Owner</th><td><a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Website</th><td class="url"><span class="url"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com">books<wbr />.google<wbr />.com</a></span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Launched</th><td>October&#160;2004<span class="noprint">&#59;&#32;14&#160;years ago</span><span style="display:none">&#160;(<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2004-10</span>)</span> (as Google Print)</td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Current&#160;status</th><td class="category">Active</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Google Books</b> (previously known as <b>Google Book Search</b> and <b>Google Print</b> and by its codename <b>Project Ocean</b>)<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> is a service from <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google Inc.</a> that searches the full text of books and magazines that Google has scanned, converted to text using <a href="/wiki/Optical_character_recognition" title="Optical character recognition">optical character recognition</a> (OCR), and stored in its digital database.<sup id="cite_ref-GoogleLinks_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GoogleLinks-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Books are provided either by publishers and authors through the Google Books Partner Program, or by Google's library partners through the Library Project.<sup id="cite_ref-book_sources_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-book_sources-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Additionally, Google has partnered with a number of magazine publishers to digitize their archives.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-magazines_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-magazines-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Publisher Program was first known as Google Print when it was introduced at the <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt_Book_Fair" title="Frankfurt Book Fair">Frankfurt Book Fair</a> in October 2004. The Google Books Library Project, which scans works in the collections of library partners and adds them to the digital inventory, was announced in December 2004.
</p><p>The Google Books initiative has been hailed for its potential to offer unprecedented access to what may become the largest online body of human knowledge<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> and promoting the <a href="/wiki/Democratization_of_knowledge" title="Democratization of knowledge">democratization of knowledge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-spiegel_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-spiegel-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
However, it has also been criticized for potential copyright violations,<sup id="cite_ref-spiegel_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-spiegel-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LAWSUITS_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LAWSUITS-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> and lack of editing to correct the many errors introduced into the scanned texts by the OCR process.
</p><p>As of October&#160;2015<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Google_Books&amp;action=edit">&#91;update&#93;</a></sup>, the number of scanned book titles was over 25 million, but the <a href="/wiki/Book_scanning" title="Book scanning">scanning process</a> has slowed down in American academic libraries.<sup id="cite_ref-nytimes.com_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nytimes.com-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Google estimated in 2010 that there were about 130 million distinct titles in the world,<sup id="cite_ref-PCWORLD_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PCWORLD-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> and stated that it intended to scan all of them.<sup id="cite_ref-PCWORLD_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PCWORLD-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
